<p><b>Eritrea</b> (<span class="nowrap"><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English" title="Help:IPA for English">/</a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="/ˌ/ secondary stress follows" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ˌ</span></a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="/ɛr/ 'err' in 'merry'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ɛr</span></a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="/ɨ/ 'e' in 'roses'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ɨ</span></a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="/ˈ/ primary stress follows" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ˈ</span></a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="'t' in 'tie'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">t</span></a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="'r' in 'rye'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">r</span></a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="/eɪ/ long 'a' in 'base'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">eɪ</span></a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="/./ syllable break" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">.</span></a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="/ə/ 'a' in 'about'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ə</span></a></span><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English" title="Help:IPA for English">/</a></span></span> or <span class="nowrap"><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English" title="Help:IPA for English">/</a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="/ˌ/ secondary stress follows" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ˌ</span></a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="/ɛr/ 'err' in 'merry'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ɛr</span></a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="/ɨ/ 'e' in 'roses'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ɨ</span></a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="/ˈ/ primary stress follows" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ˈ</span></a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="'t' in 'tie'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">t</span></a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="'r' in 'rye'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">r</span></a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="/iː/ long 'e' in 'bead'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">iː</span></a></span><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Help:IPA for English"><span title="/ə/ 'a' in 'about'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ə</span></a></span><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English" title="Help:IPA for English">/</a></span></span>;<sup id="cite_ref-:0_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-7"><span>[</span>7<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Tigrinya_language" title="Tigrinya language">Tigrinya</a>: <span lang="ti">ኤርትራ</span><a href="/wiki/Help:Multilingual_support_(Ethiopic)" title="Help:Multilingual support (Ethiopic)"><sup><span class="t nihongo icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></sup></a> <i><span title="Tigrinya transliteration" class="Unicode" style="white-space:normal; text-decoration: none">ʾErtrā </span></i>; <a href="/wiki/Arabic_language" title="Arabic language">Arabic</a>: <span lang="ar">إرتريا</span>‎ <i><span title="ar ALA transliteration" class="Unicode" style="white-space:normal; text-decoration: none">Iritriyā</span></i>), officially the <b>State of Eritrea</b>,<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8"><span>[</span>8<span>]</span></a></sup> is a country in the <a href="/wiki/Horn_of_Africa" title="Horn of Africa">Horn of Africa</a>. With its capital at <a href="/wiki/Asmara" title="Asmara">Asmara</a>, it is bordered by <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a> in the west, <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a> in the south, and <a href="/wiki/Djibouti" title="Djibouti">Djibouti</a> in the southeast. The northeastern and eastern parts of Eritrea have an extensive coastline along the <a href="/wiki/Red_Sea" title="Red Sea">Red Sea</a>, across from <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a>. The nation has a total area of approximately 117,600&#160;km<sup>2</sup> (45,406&#160;sq&#160;mi), and includes the <a href="/wiki/Dahlak_Archipelago" title="Dahlak Archipelago">Dahlak Archipelago</a> and several of the <a href="/wiki/Hanish_Islands" title="Hanish Islands">Hanish Islands</a>. Its name <i>Eritrea</i> is based on the <a href="/wiki/Greek_language" title="Greek language">Greek</a> name for the Red Sea (<span lang="grc">Ἐρυθρὰ Θάλασσα <i>Erythra Thalassa</i></span>), which was first adopted for <a href="/wiki/Italian_Eritrea" title="Italian Eritrea">Italian Eritrea</a> in 1890.</p>
<p>Eritrea is a multi-ethnic country, with nine recognized ethnic groups. It has a population of around six million inhabitants. Most residents speak <a href="/wiki/Afroasiatic_languages" title="Afroasiatic languages">Afroasiatic languages</a>, either of the <a href="/wiki/Semitic_languages" title="Semitic languages">Semitic</a> or <a href="/wiki/Cushitic_languages" title="Cushitic languages">Cushitic</a> branches. Among these communities, the <a href="/wiki/Tigray-Tigrinya_people" title="Tigray-Tigrinya people">Tigrinya</a> make up about 55% of the population, with the <a href="/wiki/Tigre_people" title="Tigre people">Tigre people</a> constituting around 30% of inhabitants. In addition, there are a number of <a href="/wiki/Nilo-Saharan_languages" title="Nilo-Saharan languages">Nilo-Saharan</a>-speaking <a href="/wiki/Nilotic" title="Nilotic" class="mw-redirect">Nilotic</a> ethnic minorities. Most people in the territory adhere to <a href="/wiki/Christianity" title="Christianity">Christianity</a> or <a href="/wiki/Islam" title="Islam">Islam</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-CIA_1-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CIA-1"><span>[</span>1<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Aksum" title="Kingdom of Aksum">Kingdom of Aksum</a>, covering much of modern-day Eritrea and <a href="/wiki/Tigray_Region" title="Tigray Region">northern Ethiopia</a>, rose somewhere around the first or second centuries<sup id="cite_ref-Munro-Hay57_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Munro-Hay57-9"><span>[</span>9<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Paul_B._Henze_2005_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Paul_B._Henze_2005-10"><span>[</span>10<span>]</span></a></sup> and adopted <a href="/wiki/Eritrean_Orthodox_Church" title="Eritrean Orthodox Church" class="mw-redirect">Christianity</a> around the time Islam had spread through Egypt and the Levant.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11"><span>[</span>11<span>]</span></a></sup> In medieval times much of Eritrea fell under the <a href="/wiki/Medri_Bahri" title="Medri Bahri">Medri Bahri Kingdom</a>, with a smaller region being part of <a href="/wiki/Hamasien" title="Hamasien">the Hamasien Republic</a>. The creation of modern day Eritrea is a result of the incorporation of independent Kingdoms and various vassal states of the Ethiopian empire and the <a href="/wiki/Habesh" title="Habesh" class="mw-redirect">Ottoman Empire</a>, eventually resulting in the formation of <a href="/wiki/Italian_Eritrea" title="Italian Eritrea">Italian Eritrea</a>. In 1947 Eritrea became part of a federation with Ethiopia, the <a href="/wiki/Federation_of_Ethiopia_and_Eritrea" title="Federation of Ethiopia and Eritrea">Federation of Ethiopia and Eritrea</a>. Subsequent <a href="/wiki/Annexation" title="Annexation">annexation</a> into Ethiopia led to the <a href="/wiki/Eritrean_War_of_Independence" title="Eritrean War of Independence">Eritrean War of Independence</a>, ending with Eritrean independence following a <a href="/wiki/Eritrean_independence_referendum,_1993" title="Eritrean independence referendum, 1993">referendum</a> in April 1993. Hostilities between Eritrea and Ethiopia persisted, leading to the <a href="/wiki/Eritrean%E2%80%93Ethiopian_War" title="Eritrean–Ethiopian War">Eritrean–Ethiopian War</a> of 1998–2000 and further skirmishes with both <a href="/wiki/Djiboutian%E2%80%93Eritrean_border_conflict" title="Djiboutian–Eritrean border conflict">Djibouti</a> and <a href="/wiki/2010_Eritrean%E2%80%93Ethiopian_border_skirmish" title="2010 Eritrean–Ethiopian border skirmish">Ethiopia</a>.</p>
<p>Eritrea is a member of the <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a>, the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> and <a href="/wiki/IGAD" title="IGAD" class="mw-redirect">IGAD</a>, and is an observer in the <a href="/wiki/Arab_League" title="Arab League">Arab League</a>.</p>
<p></p>
